### Cursor Outcome

Independent outcome_review: 16 plan-owned files present (13 modified + 3 new); P1?P7 source wiring and autonomy-stops-at-draft confirmed; all 11 traceability tests pass live under Python 3.13. Residual gap is regression-suite breadth and Postgres behavioral parity, not focused wiring correctness.

- Phase W wiring is present in the 16 plan-owned files with correct lifecycle hooks
- All 11 traceability tests pass when executed with Python >=3.10
- Autonomy stops at draft: automatic paths create draft experiments/proposals; only operator activate/approve/deny mutates execution/policy state
- P7 request-path guard is non-vacuous (AssertionError seams on dispatcher run_once and subprocess.Popen)

- accept

- None recorded.
